Benchmarks

Benchmark Evidence, Not a Leaderboard

The website renders committed static artifacts. Benchmark timing is interpreted beside the generated current-support matrix instead of restating support posture here.

Current support source

Benchmarks reuse the status matrix.

Runtime support counts come from docs/status/runs-today-support-matrix.json. The benchmark artifact supplies timing and coverage context; it is not the source of truth for support claims.

33support rows
18executable
5feature-gated
5claim/platform blocked

Support claim boundary: current-state discoverability only; this matrix does not expand runtime support or authorize production, package, performance, object-store, lakehouse, Foundry, REST, or Spark-replacement claims.

Public front doors

Route rows name the user-facing prepared paths.

The benchmark bundle publishes route-identity rows for the high-level Python front doors. These rows are not timing rows; they bind the public surface to the route lane, preparation boundary, reuse manifest, and no-fallback posture.

Front door not_timing_row_route_identity_only

ctx.prepare_vortex('fact.csv', dim='dim.csv', workspace='target/shardloom-prepared').query('selective filter').collect()

Route timing dashboard

Route lanes are the comparison surface.

Stage pieces explain a ShardLoom route; they are not competing product lanes. Warm prepared and native Vortex rows stay labeled by start state.

Stage attribution

ShardLoom stage pieces explain route cost.

Preparation, query, output, evidence, and diagnostic context are separated from route-level comparisons so a warm prepared slice cannot be read as a cold end-to-end route. The refreshed safe-writer artifact keeps exclusive stage timing visible for source read/parse, the inclusive import audit bundle, and workspace-safe Vortex write timing; the active child execution queue now records writer metadata coalescing, projection-aware text decode, source-admission packets, row-assembly strategy evidence, JSONL fast-path tail skipping, prepared-state lookup timing evidence, and result-sink capillary evidence before evidence rendering.

RouteRowsSource admissionSource readParse/decodeSource -> Vortex arrayVortex writeVortex reopen/verifyPrepared lookup/createVortex scanOperator computeResult sinkEvidence renderTotal route
ShardLoom Prepare-Once First Query12042.01 msn/a4.06 ms0.01 ms32.71 msn/a51.84 ms0.26 ms0.26 ms1.96 ms2.57 ms58.00 ms
ShardLoom Prepare-Once Batch12042.01 msn/a0.20 ms0.00 ms1.64 msn/a2.59 ms0.26 ms0.26 ms1.96 ms2.57 ms8.37 ms
ShardLoom Cold Certified Route120n/a7.80 ms29.48 msn/a76.79 msn/an/a2.32 msn/a1.90 ms0.08 ms137.71 ms
ShardLoom Warm Prepared Query12042.47 msn/an/an/an/an/an/a0.26 ms0.26 ms2.02 ms2.46 ms5.57 ms
ShardLoom Native Vortex Query12042.21 msn/an/an/an/an/an/a0.25 ms0.25 ms2.05 ms2.42 ms5.58 ms

Schema: shardloom.website.route_runtime_status.v1. Boundary: stage attribution explains why a ShardLoom route took time; stage pieces are not competing product lanes.

Route-share attribution

Optimization targets follow route share.

Route totals remain the comparison surface. The Amdahl table identifies the largest measured stage per ShardLoom route, while source-read scout and Vortex reopen/scan tables show which split evidence is complete or still blocked before stronger optimization claims.

Runtime fast path

Runtime timing is separate from output and evidence rendering.

Sub-ms prepared/native query work can coexist with larger sink or evidence-render costs because route timing, output delivery, evidence capture, and certificate linkage are reported as separate buckets.

Artifact table: Runtime Fast Path Versus Evidence Path.

RouteRowsRuntime executionOutput deliveryEvidence captureEvidence renderCertificate linkEvidence render route totalCertificate status

Schema: shardloom.route_fast_path_attribution.v1. Boundary: runtime execution timing, output delivery, evidence capture, evidence render, and certificate linking are separate interpretation buckets; fast-path timing is not a performance superiority claim.

Evidence-render proof

Human benchmark evidence is regenerated from compact facts.

Evidence-render proof fields carry compact route facts, digest evidence, no-fallback markers, and a claim boundary so the promoter and website can expand human tables outside the hot Rust route. Current route timing values stay unchanged until the benchmark suite is rerun.

Artifact table: Evidence-Render Proof Regeneration.

StatusRowsRoutesRoute timing boundaryHot-path policyHuman expansion timingDigest sample
compact_machine_evidence_derived600ShardLoom Cold Certified Route, ShardLoom Native Vortex Query, ShardLoom Prepare-Once Batch, ShardLoom Prepare-Once First Query, ShardLoom Warm Prepared Queryroute_total_includes_evidence_render_timingcompact_facts_only_human_render_deferredoutside_timed_route_promoter_or_website_rendersha256:f4c08abd2a6423b3

Schema: shardloom.traditional_analytics.evidence_render_proof.v1. Proof rows in current artifact: 1320. Boundary: compact evidence-render proof fields support benchmark attribution and website/table regeneration only; route totals remain the comparison surface and no performance, production, package, SQL/DataFrame, object-store/lakehouse, Foundry, or Spark-displacement claim is authorized.

Result-sink capillary

Native result output is separated from compatibility fanout.

Requested result sinks now carry scalar JSON byte/digest evidence, native Vortex output selection, compatibility fanout selection, replay digest parity, and explicit no-fallback fields. The current public artifact predates those fields, so route timing values stay unchanged until the benchmark suite is rerun.

RouteScenarioStatusCapillary routeJSON bytesNative VortexCompat fanoutDigestNo fallback
Awaiting refreshed benchmark artifact after the current optimization batch.

Capillary rows in current artifact: 0. Rust emits the new `result_sink_capillary_*` fields; public route timing values stay unchanged until the benchmark suite is rerun.

Operator mode inventory

Runtime support is not encoded-native support.

Rows can be scoped-runtime-supported while their operators remain residual-native or materialized-temporary. Encoded-native execution is a separate claim with its own blocker code and promotion candidate.

Prepare-once reuse

Amortization is shown as route math.

The prepared route keeps first-query cost visible, then shows how the same preparation cost amortizes across repeated prepared executions. Refreshed artifacts can also expose prepared-state manifest lookup, cache hit, miss-create, artifact write, register, replay verification, and attractor-key evidence.

Current artifact profile: full_local. Lane availability is generated by the benchmark promoter. The current full_local profile compares ShardLoom against local non-Spark baselines; full_local_plus_spark is the explicit-only Spark profile for pyspark, spark-default, and spark-local-tuned. Spark lanes are explicit-only historical baselines. Performance claim allowed: false. Benchmark constitution claim gate: not_claim_grade. Claim boundary: local_comparative_broad_formats_not_claim_grade.

Benchmark constitution

Rows need route, correctness, environment, and no-fallback proof before claims.

The manifest names the row validator and the field set required before any benchmark row can become claim-grade. Current static artifacts remain interpretation evidence, not public performance claims.

Schema
shardloom.benchmark_constitution_validation.v1
Validator
scripts/check_benchmark_constitution.py
Claim gate
not_claim_grade
Performance claim allowed
false

Required row fields: benchmark_result_row, route_identity, route_runtime_status, dataset_source_admission, preparation_route, execution_route, output_route, claim_readiness_boundary, correctness_proof, hardware_profile, build_profile, cold_warm_state, stage_timings, route_timing_ledger, cold_lane_attribution, cost_unit_fields, no_fallback_proof, external_baseline_boundary.

Cold-lane attribution

Cold ingest bottlenecks stay attached to the route.

The promoter classifies each row before publication and labels the dominant cold-stage bottleneck. Missing stage splits block claim-grade interpretation instead of letting cold preparation or harness overhead hide inside a single timing number. The page should be refreshed with the post-optimization artifact whenever source-normalization or writer-stage code changes land.

Format coverage

CSV and Parquet are not the whole target roster.

The published artifact now shows expected broad-format coverage instead of making absent JSONL, Arrow IPC, Avro, or ORC rows look irrelevant.

Runtime status

Runtime support is separate from claim readiness.

A row can be scoped-runtime-supported without authorizing performance, production, or Spark-replacement claims. External unsupported rows are baseline limitations, not ShardLoom runtime gaps.

ScopeRowsInterpretation
ShardLoom unsupported rows0ShardLoom runtime gaps in the promoted comparative roster
External baseline unsupported rows6External engine limitation rows; not ShardLoom runtime gaps
route_runtime_status=external_baseline_only720published row status vocabulary
route_runtime_status=scoped_runtime_supported600published row status vocabulary

Status vocabulary: external_baseline_only, feature_gated, fixture_smoke_only, scoped_runtime_supported, unsupported.

Claim-gate distribution

Evidence quality is not the same as runtime support.

Timing rows remain local context, not superiority proof. Compatibility cold timing is not pure query speed. Runtime support, evidence quality, and claim authorization are shown as separate layers.

external_baseline_only714 rows - 54.1%
claim_grade600 rows - 45.5%
unsupported6 rows - 0.5%
Prepared/native source-state evidence rows2 batch rows
Published comparative roster1320 rows

Claim-grade closeout

ShardLoom gaps and external baseline limits are counted separately.

This page keeps runtime status, evidence quality, and claim authorization separate. External baseline unsupported rows do not imply a ShardLoom route gap.

ScopeCurrent rowsTargetPlan item
ShardLoom runtime rows600 rows; 0 not claim-grade/blocked/unsupported/fixture rowsclaim_grade for every admitted row in the published comparative profileGAR-RUNTIME-IMPL-5J
External baseline rowsexternal_baseline_only rows remain comparison contextvisible baseline-only rows; never fallback executionGAR-BENCH-PUB-1 / GAR-RUNTIME-IMPL-5J
ShardLoom unsupported rows0 ShardLoom rows0 ShardLoom unsupported rows in the admitted benchmark-range route rosterGAR-RUNTIME-IMPL-6D
External baseline unsupported rows6 external baseline rowsvisible baseline engine limitation rows; never counted as ShardLoom runtime gapsGAR-BENCH-PUB-1 / GAR-RUNTIME-IMPL-6D
